	jQuery("#main_search_form input[type='text']").rb_text( { enable_border: true, border_color: rb2_components_theme_color, hover_border_color: rb2_components_theme_color } );	
	
	jQuery("#main_search_form select").rb_select( { color: "#828282", enable_border: false } );	
	
	jQuery("#main_search_form .range_element").rb_range( { color: "#828282", changed: function( ){ 
															resultCounter( );
															// clearTimeout( rb_range_change_timer );
														 	// rb_range_change_timer = setTimeout( function( ){ resultCounter( ); }, 1000);  
															
														} } ); 
														
	jQuery("#main_search_form input[type='radio']").rb_radio( { color: "#828282" } );
	
	jQuery("#main_search_form .su7cs_search_btn_submit").rb_button(  );		
	
	
	jQuery(".rb2_text i.fa-search").click( function( ){ jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").click( ); } );
	
});

</script>

}</style><script>/* 
 * To change this license header, choose License Headers in Project Properties.
 * To change this template file, choose Tools | Templates
 * and open the template in the editor.
 */
   var result_timer = null;
   var firstload = 0;
   	
   jQuery(document).ready(function(){
	   
	    jQuery(window).on("load", function(){
			
			startBoxCorrector( );
			
			setTimeout( function( ){ imageContainerHeightSet( ); }, 1000 );				
			sendChangeEvents( );			
			
		});
	   
			jQuery("#adv_search_order_by").change(function(){
				
				jQuery("#main_search_form").submit( );
				
			});
	   
			if ( jQuery("#s_string").val( ).length > 0 ){
				disableForm( true );
			}else{
				disableForm( false );
			}	
   
			jQuery("#s_string").keyup( function( ){
				
				if ( jQuery(this).val( ).trim().length > 0 ){
					disableForm( true );
				}else{
					disableForm( false );
				}			
				
			});
			
			result_timer = setTimeout( function( ){
					
					resultCounter( );
					
				}, 1000 );
	      
			setTimeout( function(){ check_active_reset_filter(); }, 1000 );
			
			jQuery(".su7cs_main select, .su7cs_main input[type='radio']").change( function(){
				
				check_active_reset_filter();
				
				clearTimeout( result_timer );
				
				result_timer = setTimeout( function( ){
					
					resultCounter( );
					
				}, 500 );								
				
			});		
   
			jQuery(".car_search_filter_reset").click(function(){
				
				jQuery(".su7cs_main select").each(function(){
					jQuery(this).prop('selectedIndex',0);
				});
				
				jQuery(".car_search_filter_reset").prop('disabled', true);
				
			});
                        
            jQuery("select[data-join]").each(function(){
                
              var this_select =  jQuery(this);
                
              fix_join_element_value( this_select );
                
              var join_target = "search_" + this_select.attr("data-join");
             
              join_target = jQuery("select[name='" + join_target + "']");
                           
              if ( join_target.val() == "" ){  
                 this_select.prop('disabled', true);
              }
              
              
                  
              check_options( this_select, join_target.val()  );
             
              
              join_target.change(function(){                    
				  		  
					  // reset_option(this_select);
					  check_options( this_select, jQuery(this).val()  );                  
                
              });
               
                if ( join_target.find("option").length == 2 && this_select.find("option:selected").index() == 0 ){
                    
                    join_target.find("option").last().prop( "selected", true );
					join_target.trigger("change");
					firstload += 1;
                    
                }
                
            });
			
			function sendChangeEvents(){
			
				jQuery("select[data-join]").each(function(){
					
					var name = "search_" + jQuery(this).attr("data-join");				
					check_options( jQuery(this), jQuery("select[name='" + name + "']").val( ) );				
					
				});
				
				return true;
			}
				
            function check_options( p_element, value  ){
                
                 if ( value != "" ){
					                     
					 jQuery("#" + p_element.attr("uniq_id") ).removeClass("rb2_disabled");
					 
                     find_match_options( p_element, value );                    
                     find_match_rb2_select( jQuery("#" + p_element.attr("uniq_id") ), value );                    
                     p_element.prop('disabled', false);                     
                      
                  }else{                      
                      
					  setTimeout( function(){
							
							jQuery("#" + p_element.attr("uniq_id") ).find(".list ul > li").not(":first").hide();
							jQuery("#" + p_element.attr("uniq_id") ).find(".list ul > li").first().click().click();
							jQuery("#" + p_element.attr("uniq_id") ).addClass("rb2_disabled");
							
					  }, 100 );
					  
                      p_element.prop('disabled', true);
                      
                  }
                
            }
            
            function reset_option( this_select ){
                this_select.find("option:selected").removeAttr("selected");
                this_select.find("option").first().prop('selected', true); 
            }
			
			function find_match_rb2_select( element, val ){
				
				element.find(".list ul > li").show( );
				
				element.find(".list ul > li").each( function(){
					
				   var curr_val = jQuery(this).attr("join-val");
				   console.log( "-->
        " + val + " : " + curr_val );				  
				   if ( curr_val == val  ){					   
						jQuery(this).show();						
					}else{
						jQuery(this).hide();
					}
					
				} );
				
				if( element.find(".list ul &gt; li.selected-item:visible").length != 0 ){
					element.find(".list ul &gt; li.selected-item:visible").show().click().click();
				}else{
					element.find(".list ul &gt; li:first").show().click().click();
				}
							
				return true;
			}
            
            function find_match_options( element, val ){
                
                element.find("option").each(function(){
                    
                    var curr_val = jQuery(this).attr("join-val");
                   
                   if ( val != null ){
                       if ( curr_val.toString().toLowerCase() == val.toString().toLowerCase() || jQuery(this).val() == ""  ){                       
                            jQuery(this).show();
                        }else{
                             jQuery(this).hide();
                        }
                   }else{
                       jQuery(this).hide();
                   }
                    
                    
                });
                
            }
            
            
            function fix_join_element_value( element ){
                
                element.find("option").each(function(){
                    
                    var v = jQuery(this).text();
                    var sp_value = v.toString().split(':');
                    jQuery(this).attr("join-val", sp_value[0] );
                    jQuery(this).val(sp_value[1]);
                    jQuery(this).text(sp_value[1]);
                    
                });
                                
            }
            
        });
             		
		function startBoxCorrector(){
			
			setTimeout(function(){
				
				if ( jQuery("#posts-container").first().height() == 0 ){
					
					startBoxCorrector();
					
				}else{
											
					setTimeout( function(){ 
					
						set_inLine_height(); 
						set_cel_height();
						set_grid_container();
						fix_grid_cel_top(); 
					
					}, 500 );
					
				}
				
            },500);
					  
			
		}
		
		var grid_top_margin = 30;
						
		function set_cel_height(){
			
			var h = 0;
			
			jQuery( ".fusion-post-grid .fusion-column-wrapper" ).each( function(){
								
				if ( h &lt; jQuery(this).height()){
					h = jQuery(this).height();
				}							
				
			});			
			
			jQuery( ".fusion-post-grid .fusion-column-wrapper" ).height( h );
			
		}
				
		function set_grid_container(){
			//fusion-blog-layout-grid
			var max_h = 0;
			var first_left = jQuery( ".fusion-post-grid" ).each(function(){
				
				var h=0;
				var first_left = jQuery( this ).css("left");
				jQuery( ".fusion-post-grid" ).each( function(){
					
					if ( jQuery( this ).css("left") == first_left ){
						h += jQuery( this ).height() + grid_top_margin;
					}
					
				});
				
				if ( h &gt; max_h ){
					
					max_h = h;
					
				}
				
			});
			
			jQuery(".fusion-blog-layout-grid").height( max_h );
			
		}
		
		function check_active_reset_filter(){
			
			var selected_filter = true;
			 
			jQuery(".su7cs_main select").each(function(){
				
				if ( jQuery(this).prop('selectedIndex') != 0 ){
					
						selected_filter = false;
						
				}
					
			});
			
			jQuery(".car_search_filter_reset").prop('disabled', selected_filter);
			
			return selected_filter;
			
		}
		
		function fix_grid_cel_top(){
			
			var counter = 0;

			jQuery( "body.blog .fusion-post-grid" ).each( function(){

					var main_cel = jQuery( this );
					var this_left = main_cel.css("left");		
					var bottom = 0;
					
					jQuery( this ).nextAll( ".fusion-post-grid" ).each(function(){

							if ( jQuery( this ).css("left") == this_left ){
									
									bottom +=  main_cel.height() + grid_top_margin;
									
									jQuery( this ).css("top", bottom + "px");

							}

					});

					counter ++;

					if ( counter == 3 ){
						   return false;
					}

			} );

		}
		
		function set_inLine_height(){
			
			var maxHeight = -1;
			
			jQuery(".fusion-one-full &gt; .fusion-column-wrapper &gt; .cardRibbon + .cardContent").each(function(){
				
				 maxHeight = maxHeight &gt; jQuery(this).height() ? maxHeight : jQuery(this).height();
				
			});
			
			// var fix_top = 0;
			
			jQuery(".fusion-one-full &gt; .fusion-column-wrapper &gt; .cardRibbon + .cardContent").height( maxHeight );
			
			maxHeight = -1;
			
			jQuery(".fusion-one-full &gt; .fusion-column-wrapper &gt; .cardContent.consumptionList").each(function(){
				
				 maxHeight = maxHeight &gt; jQuery(this).height() ? maxHeight : jQuery(this).height();
				
			});
			
			jQuery(".fusion-one-full &gt; .fusion-column-wrapper &gt; .cardContent.consumptionList").height( maxHeight );
			
			// jQuery(".fusion-one-full &gt; .fusion-column-wrapper &gt; .cardRibbon + .cardContent").each( function(){
				
				// fix_top = maxHeight - jQuery(this).height();
				// jQuery(this).height( maxHeight );	
				// jQuery(this).find(".car-inf-div").css({"top" : fix_top + "px"});
				
			// } );					
					
		}
        		
		function resultCounter( ){				
			
			var submitForm = jQuery( "#main_search_form" );

			var submitContainer = submitForm.find("button[type='submit']").parent("div");

			submitContainer.addClass("search-submit-container");			

			submitForm.find(".car_search_filter_reset").click(function(){

					setTimeout( function(){ getNewResultCount( submitContainer, submitForm ); }, 200 );	

			});
			
			getNewResultCount( submitContainer, submitForm );
			
			return true;
		}
		
		var cachedNewResultCount = [ ];
		
		function getNewResultCount( element, submitForm ){
		
			var submitForm = jQuery( "#main_search_form" );
			
			element.find("button").html(getResultCountText('
        <i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-spinner fa-spin">
        </i>
        '));
			
			var url = submitForm.attr("action") + "?q=true&amp;" + submitForm.serialize( ) ; //+ "&amp;v=" + Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000)
		
			var cachedData = checkExistCachedUrl( url );
			// console.log( url );
			// cachedData = false; ////////////   IGNORE CACHE
			
			$effect = "flipInX";
			
			$baseEffect = "bounceInFix";
			
			if( !jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").attr("animated") ){
				jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").addClass("animated");
				jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").attr("animated", "true");
			}
						
			jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").removeClass($effect);
			jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").removeClass($baseEffect);
		
			setTimeout( function( ){ 
			
				jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").addClass($effect);
				
				setTimeout( function( ){ 
				
					jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").removeClass($effect);
					jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").addClass($baseEffect);									
				
				}, 1000);
			
			}, 100 );
			
			if ( cachedData !== false ){
								
				// setResultCount( element, cachedData );
				setResultCount( element, cachedData );
				
				
								
			}else{				
				
				jQuery.get( url + "&amp;v=" + Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000), function( data ){ 
				
					setResultCount( element, data );
					cachedNewResultCount[ cachedNewResultCount.length ] = { "url" : url, "data" : data };					
					// console.log( cachedNewResultCount );					
					

				});	
				
			}
			
			return true;
		}
		
		function setResultCount( element, data ){
			
			element.find("button").html(getResultCountText(data)); 
			return true;
			
		}
		
		function getResultCountText( text ){
			return '
        <i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-search">
        </i>
        <span class="result-text">
         <span class="result-quantity">
          ' + text + '
         </span>
         Angebote
        </span>
        ';
		}
		
		function checkExistCachedUrl( url ){
			
			for( var i = 0; i &lt; cachedNewResultCount.length; i++ ){
								
				if ( cachedNewResultCount[ i ].url == url ){
					
					return cachedNewResultCount[ i ].data;
					break;
					
				}
				
			}
			
			return false;
		}
		
		function disableForm( $show ){
			
			if( jQuery( "#search_main_container .su7cs_main .disabled_form" ).length == 0  )
				jQuery( "#search_main_container .su7cs_main" ).append( "
        <div class="disabled_form">
        </div>
        " );
			
			if ( $show ){
				jQuery( "#search_main_container .su7cs_main .disabled_form" ).show( );
			}else{
				jQuery( "#search_main_container .su7cs_main .disabled_form" ).hide( );
			}
			
		}
		
		
		function imageContainerHeightSet( ){
			
			var maxH = 0;
			
			jQuery( "#posts-container a.car-img-content" ).each( function( ){
				
				if ( maxH &lt; jQuery(this).height( ) )
					maxH = jQuery(this).height( );
				
			} );
			
			jQuery( "#posts-container a.car-img-content" ).height( maxH );
			
		}

        <div class="fusion-title title fusion-sep-none fusion-title-size-one" style="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:20px;">
         <h1 class="title-heading-left">
          <strong>
           Autozentrum Epple − Günstige Neuwagen und Gebrauchtwagen in Rutesheim &amp; Weil der Stadt
          </strong>
         </h1>
        </div>
        <p>
         Ihr Fahrzeug-Partner für die Marken Ford, Mazda, Volvo &amp; Suzuki.
        </p>
        <p>
         Das Autozentrum Epple, Ihr Vertragshändler für Ford, Mazda, Volvo &amp; Suzuki in Rutesheim &amp; Weil der Stadt, stellt sich, seine Leistungen und seinen tagesaktuellen Fahrzeugbestand vor. Ob Neu oder Gebraucht-Fahrzeuge: Wir vermitteln Ihnen die Serienmodelle aller Fahrzeugreihen.
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         Mit unserem erstklassigen Service sorgen wir für die Mobilität Ihrer Fahrzeuge. Ihr Fahrzeug ist bei uns in Besten Händen. Überzeugen Sie sich selbst und vereinbaren Sie noch heute einen
         <strong>
          <a href="/service/terminvereinbarung/">
           Termin »
          </a>
         </strong>
        </p>
        <div class="fusion-sep-clear">
        </div>

      </div>

  <script>
   jQuery(document).ready(function(){
    
    if ( jQuery("[data-target='.f_tool']").length != 0 ){
        
        jQuery("[data-target='.f_tool']").click(function(){
            
            var url =  jQuery("#f_tool_object").attr("url-data");
            var price = Math.floor(jQuery(this).attr("data-price"));
            var version = Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000);
          
            jQuery("#f_tool_object").attr("data", url + "?f_p=" + price + "&v="  + version);
            
        });
        
    }
    
    if( jQuery("#data_privacy").length != 0 ){
        
       setTimeout(function(){
           
            var regex = /(\?|\&)f_p=(.*?)($|&)/g;
            var str = window.location.href;
            
            var reg = new RegExp( regex );   
            var result;
            while (result = reg.exec(str)){
                match = result[2];
                jQuery("#total_price_input").val(match);
                jQuery("#total_price_input").trigger("change");

            } 
                
       }, 100);
        
    };
    
});
  </script>

  <script>
   jQuery(document).ready(function () {
        appendPath();
        insertSubject();

    })


    function appendPath() {
        if (jQuery('.customButton').length) {
            jQuery('.customButton').each(function() {
                var oldHref = jQuery(this).attr('href').replace('origin', '');
                var path = window.location.pathname;

                jQuery(this).attr('href', oldHref + path);
            })
        }
    }

    function insertSubject() {
        if (jQuery('.betreff').length) {
            var input = jQuery('.betreff > input');
			
            var origin = toTitleCase(window.location.hash.replace("#/", "").replace(/\//g, " » ").slice(0, -3).replace( /\%20/g , ' ' ));

            input.val(origin);
        }

    }

    function toTitleCase(str) {
        return str.replace(/\w\S*/g, function(txt){return txt.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + txt.substr(1).toLowerCase();});
    }
  </script>

    var result_timer = null;
    var firstload = 0;
    	
    jQuery(document).ready(function(){
 	   
 	    jQuery(window).on("load", function(){
 			
 			startBoxCorrector( );
 			
 			setTimeout( function( ){ imageContainerHeightSet( ); }, 1000 );				
 			sendChangeEvents( );			
 			
 		});
 	   
 			jQuery("#adv_search_order_by").change(function(){
 				
 				jQuery("#main_search_form").submit( );
 				
 			});
 	   
 			if ( jQuery("#s_string").val( ).length > 0 ){
 				disableForm( true );
 			}else{
 				disableForm( false );
 			}	
    
 			jQuery("#s_string").keyup( function( ){
 				
 				if ( jQuery(this).val( ).trim().length > 0 ){
 					disableForm( true );
 				}else{
 					disableForm( false );
 				}			
 				
 			});
 			
 			result_timer = setTimeout( function( ){
 					
 					resultCounter( );
 					
 				}, 1000 );
 	      
 			setTimeout( function(){ check_active_reset_filter(); }, 1000 );
 			
 			jQuery(".su7cs_main select, .su7cs_main input[type='radio']").change( function(){
 				
 				check_active_reset_filter();
 				
 				clearTimeout( result_timer );
 				
 				result_timer = setTimeout( function( ){
 					
 					resultCounter( );
 					
 				}, 500 );								
 				
 			});		
    
 			jQuery(".car_search_filter_reset").click(function(){
 				
 				jQuery(".su7cs_main select").each(function(){
 					jQuery(this).prop('selectedIndex',0);
 				});
 				
 				jQuery(".car_search_filter_reset").prop('disabled', true);
 				
 			});
                         
             jQuery("select[data-join]").each(function(){
                 
               var this_select =  jQuery(this);
                 
               fix_join_element_value( this_select );
                 
               var join_target = "search_" + this_select.attr("data-join");
              
               join_target = jQuery("select[name='" + join_target + "']");
                            
               if ( join_target.val() == "" ){  
                  this_select.prop('disabled', true);
               }
               
               
                   
               check_options( this_select, join_target.val()  );
              
               
               join_target.change(function(){                    
 				  		  
 					  // reset_option(this_select);
 					  check_options( this_select, jQuery(this).val()  );                  
                 
               });
                
                 if ( join_target.find("option").length == 2 && this_select.find("option:selected").index() == 0 ){
                     
                     join_target.find("option").last().prop( "selected", true );
 					join_target.trigger("change");
 					firstload += 1;
                     
                 }
                 
             });
 			
 			function sendChangeEvents(){
 			
 				jQuery("select[data-join]").each(function(){
 					
 					var name = "search_" + jQuery(this).attr("data-join");				
 					check_options( jQuery(this), jQuery("select[name='" + name + "']").val( ) );				
 					
 				});
 				
 				return true;
 			}
 				
             function check_options( p_element, value  ){
                 
                  if ( value != "" ){
 					                     
 					 jQuery("#" + p_element.attr("uniq_id") ).removeClass("rb2_disabled");
 					 
                      find_match_options( p_element, value );                    
                      find_match_rb2_select( jQuery("#" + p_element.attr("uniq_id") ), value );                    
                      p_element.prop('disabled', false);                     
                       
                   }else{                      
                       
 					  setTimeout( function(){
 							
 							jQuery("#" + p_element.attr("uniq_id") ).find(".list ul > li").not(":first").hide();
 							jQuery("#" + p_element.attr("uniq_id") ).find(".list ul > li").first().click().click();
 							jQuery("#" + p_element.attr("uniq_id") ).addClass("rb2_disabled");
 							
 					  }, 100 );
 					  
                       p_element.prop('disabled', true);
                       
                   }
                 
             }
             
             function reset_option( this_select ){
                 this_select.find("option:selected").removeAttr("selected");
                 this_select.find("option").first().prop('selected', true); 
             }
 			
 			function find_match_rb2_select( element, val ){
 				
 				element.find(".list ul > li").show( );
 				
 				element.find(".list ul > li").each( function(){
 					
 				   var curr_val = jQuery(this).attr("join-val");
 				   console.log( "-->
         " + val + " : " + curr_val );				  
 				   if ( curr_val == val  ){					   
 						jQuery(this).show();						
 					}else{
 						jQuery(this).hide();
 					}
 					
 				} );
 				
 				if( element.find(".list ul &gt; li.selected-item:visible").length != 0 ){
 					element.find(".list ul &gt; li.selected-item:visible").show().click().click();
 				}else{
 					element.find(".list ul &gt; li:first").show().click().click();
 				}
 							
 				return true;
 			}
             
             function find_match_options( element, val ){
                 
                 element.find("option").each(function(){
                     
                     var curr_val = jQuery(this).attr("join-val");
                    
                    if ( val != null ){
                        if ( curr_val.toString().toLowerCase() == val.toString().toLowerCase() || jQuery(this).val() == ""  ){                       
                             jQuery(this).show();
                         }else{
                              jQuery(this).hide();
                         }
                    }else{
                        jQuery(this).hide();
                    }
                     
                     
                 });
                 
             }
             
             
             function fix_join_element_value( element ){
                 
                 element.find("option").each(function(){
                     
                     var v = jQuery(this).text();
                     var sp_value = v.toString().split(':');
                     jQuery(this).attr("join-val", sp_value[0] );
                     jQuery(this).val(sp_value[1]);
                     jQuery(this).text(sp_value[1]);
                     
                 });
                                 
             }
             
         });
              		
 		function startBoxCorrector(){
 			
 			setTimeout(function(){
 				
 				if ( jQuery("#posts-container").first().height() == 0 ){
 					
 					startBoxCorrector();
 					
 				}else{
 											
 					setTimeout( function(){ 
 					
 						set_inLine_height(); 
 						set_cel_height();
 						set_grid_container();
 						fix_grid_cel_top(); 
 					
 					}, 500 );
 					
 				}
 				
             },500);
 					  
 			
 		}
 		
 		var grid_top_margin = 30;
 						
 		function set_cel_height(){
 			
 			var h = 0;
 			
 			jQuery( ".fusion-post-grid .fusion-column-wrapper" ).each( function(){
 								
 				if ( h &lt; jQuery(this).height()){
 					h = jQuery(this).height();
 				}							
 				
 			});			
 			
 			jQuery( ".fusion-post-grid .fusion-column-wrapper" ).height( h );
 			
 		}
 				
 		function set_grid_container(){
 			//fusion-blog-layout-grid
 			var max_h = 0;
 			var first_left = jQuery( ".fusion-post-grid" ).each(function(){
 				
 				var h=0;
 				var first_left = jQuery( this ).css("left");
 				jQuery( ".fusion-post-grid" ).each( function(){
 					
 					if ( jQuery( this ).css("left") == first_left ){
 						h += jQuery( this ).height() + grid_top_margin;
 					}
 					
 				});
 				
 				if ( h &gt; max_h ){
 					
 					max_h = h;
 					
 				}
 				
 			});
 			
 			jQuery(".fusion-blog-layout-grid").height( max_h );
 			
 		}
 		
 		function check_active_reset_filter(){
 			
 			var selected_filter = true;
 			 
 			jQuery(".su7cs_main select").each(function(){
 				
 				if ( jQuery(this).prop('selectedIndex') != 0 ){
 					
 						selected_filter = false;
 						
 				}
 					
 			});
 			
 			jQuery(".car_search_filter_reset").prop('disabled', selected_filter);
 			
 			return selected_filter;
 			
 		}
 		
 		function fix_grid_cel_top(){
 			
 			var counter = 0;
 
 			jQuery( "body.blog .fusion-post-grid" ).each( function(){
 
 					var main_cel = jQuery( this );
 					var this_left = main_cel.css("left");		
 					var bottom = 0;
 					
 					jQuery( this ).nextAll( ".fusion-post-grid" ).each(function(){
 
 							if ( jQuery( this ).css("left") == this_left ){
 									
 									bottom +=  main_cel.height() + grid_top_margin;
 									
 									jQuery( this ).css("top", bottom + "px");
 
 							}
 
 					});
 
 					counter ++;
 
 					if ( counter == 3 ){
 						   return false;
 					}
 
 			} );
 
 		}
 		
 		function set_inLine_height(){
 			
 			var maxHeight = -1;
 			
 			jQuery(".fusion-one-full &gt; .fusion-column-wrapper &gt; .cardRibbon + .cardContent").each(function(){
 				
 				 maxHeight = maxHeight &gt; jQuery(this).height() ? maxHeight : jQuery(this).height();
 				
 			});
 			
 			// var fix_top = 0;
 			
 			jQuery(".fusion-one-full &gt; .fusion-column-wrapper &gt; .cardRibbon + .cardContent").height( maxHeight );
 			
 			maxHeight = -1;
 			
 			jQuery(".fusion-one-full &gt; .fusion-column-wrapper &gt; .cardContent.consumptionList").each(function(){
 				
 				 maxHeight = maxHeight &gt; jQuery(this).height() ? maxHeight : jQuery(this).height();
 				
 			});
 			
 			jQuery(".fusion-one-full &gt; .fusion-column-wrapper &gt; .cardContent.consumptionList").height( maxHeight );
 			
 			// jQuery(".fusion-one-full &gt; .fusion-column-wrapper &gt; .cardRibbon + .cardContent").each( function(){
 				
 				// fix_top = maxHeight - jQuery(this).height();
 				// jQuery(this).height( maxHeight );	
 				// jQuery(this).find(".car-inf-div").css({"top" : fix_top + "px"});
 				
 			// } );					
 					
 		}
         		
 		function resultCounter( ){				
 			
 			var submitForm = jQuery( "#main_search_form" );
 
 			var submitContainer = submitForm.find("button[type='submit']").parent("div");
 
 			submitContainer.addClass("search-submit-container");			
 
 			submitForm.find(".car_search_filter_reset").click(function(){
 
 					setTimeout( function(){ getNewResultCount( submitContainer, submitForm ); }, 200 );	
 
 			});
 			
 			getNewResultCount( submitContainer, submitForm );
 			
 			return true;
 		}
 		
 		var cachedNewResultCount = [ ];
 		
 		function getNewResultCount( element, submitForm ){
 		
 			var submitForm = jQuery( "#main_search_form" );
 			
 			element.find("button").html(getResultCountText('
         <i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-spinner fa-spin">
         </i>
         '));
 			
 			var url = submitForm.attr("action") + "?q=true&amp;" + submitForm.serialize( ) ; //+ "&amp;v=" + Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000)
 		
 			var cachedData = checkExistCachedUrl( url );
 			// console.log( url );
 			// cachedData = false; ////////////   IGNORE CACHE
 			
 			$effect = "flipInX";
 			
 			$baseEffect = "bounceInFix";
 			
 			if( !jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").attr("animated") ){
 				jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").addClass("animated");
 				jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").attr("animated", "true");
 			}
 						
 			jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").removeClass($effect);
 			jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").removeClass($baseEffect);
 		
 			setTimeout( function( ){ 
 			
 				jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").addClass($effect);
 				
 				setTimeout( function( ){ 
 				
 					jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").removeClass($effect);
 					jQuery(".su7cs_search_btn_submit").addClass($baseEffect);									
 				
 				}, 1000);
 			
 			}, 100 );
 			
 			if ( cachedData !== false ){
 								
 				// setResultCount( element, cachedData );
 				setResultCount( element, cachedData );
 				
 				
 								
 			}else{				
 				
 				jQuery.get( url + "&amp;v=" + Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000), function( data ){ 
 				
 					setResultCount( element, data );
 					cachedNewResultCount[ cachedNewResultCount.length ] = { "url" : url, "data" : data };					
 					// console.log( cachedNewResultCount );					
 					
 
 				});	
 				
 			}
 			
 			return true;
 		}
 		
 		function setResultCount( element, data ){
 			
 			element.find("button").html(getResultCountText(data)); 
 			return true;
 			
 		}
 		
 		function getResultCountText( text ){
 			return '
         <i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-search">
         </i>
         <span class="result-text">
          <span class="result-quantity">
           ' + text + '
          </span>
          Angebote
         </span>
         ';
 		}
 		
 		function checkExistCachedUrl( url ){
 			
 			for( var i = 0; i &lt; cachedNewResultCount.length; i++ ){
 								
 				if ( cachedNewResultCount[ i ].url == url ){
 					
 					return cachedNewResultCount[ i ].data;
 					break;
 					
 				}
 				
 			}
 			
 			return false;
 		}
 		
 		function disableForm( $show ){
 			
 			if( jQuery( "#search_main_container .su7cs_main .disabled_form" ).length == 0  )
 				jQuery( "#search_main_container .su7cs_main" ).append( "
         <div class="disabled_form">
         </div>
         " );
 			
 			if ( $show ){
 				jQuery( "#search_main_container .su7cs_main .disabled_form" ).show( );
 			}else{
 				jQuery( "#search_main_container .su7cs_main .disabled_form" ).hide( );
 			}
 			
 		}
 		
 		
 		function imageContainerHeightSet( ){
 			
 			var maxH = 0;
 			
 			jQuery( "#posts-container a.car-img-content" ).each( function( ){
 				
 				if ( maxH &lt; jQuery(this).height( ) )
 					maxH = jQuery(this).height( );
 				
 			} );
 			
 			jQuery( "#posts-container a.car-img-content" ).height( maxH );
 			
 		}

         <div class="fusion-title title fusion-sep-none fusion-title-size-one" style="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:20px;">
          <h1 class="title-heading-left">
           <strong>
            Autozentrum Epple − Günstige Neuwagen und Gebrauchtwagen in Rutesheim &amp; Weil der Stadt
           </strong>
          </h1>
         </div>
         <p>
          Ihr Fahrzeug-Partner für die Marken Ford, Mazda, Volvo &amp; Suzuki.
         </p>
         <p>
          Das Autozentrum Epple, Ihr Vertragshändler für Ford, Mazda, Volvo &amp; Suzuki in Rutesheim &amp; Weil der Stadt, stellt sich, seine Leistungen und seinen tagesaktuellen Fahrzeugbestand vor. Ob Neu oder Gebraucht-Fahrzeuge: Wir vermitteln Ihnen die Serienmodelle aller Fahrzeugreihen.
         </p>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p>
          Mit unserem erstklassigen Service sorgen wir für die Mobilität Ihrer Fahrzeuge. Ihr Fahrzeug ist bei uns in Besten Händen. Überzeugen Sie sich selbst und vereinbaren Sie noch heute einen
          <strong>
           <a href="/service/terminvereinbarung/">
            Termin »
           </a>
          </strong>
         </p>
         <div class="fusion-sep-clear">
         </div>

             var url =  jQuery("#f_tool_object").attr("url-data");
             var price = Math.floor(jQuery(this).attr("data-price"));
             var version = Math.floor(Math.random() * 10000000);
           
             jQuery("#f_tool_object").attr("data", url + "?f_p=" + price + "&v="  + version);
             
         });
         
     }
     
     if( jQuery("#data_privacy").length != 0 ){
         
        setTimeout(function(){
            
             var regex = /(\?|\&)f_p=(.*?)($|&)/g;
             var str = window.location.href;
             
             var reg = new RegExp( regex );   
             var result;
             while (result = reg.exec(str)){
                 match = result[2];
                 jQuery("#total_price_input").val(match);
                 jQuery("#total_price_input").trigger("change");
 
             } 
                 
        }, 100);
         
     };
     
 });
   </script>

   <script>
    jQuery(document).ready(function () {
         appendPath();
         insertSubject();
 
     })
 
 
     function appendPath() {
         if (jQuery('.customButton').length) {
             jQuery('.customButton').each(function() {
                 var oldHref = jQuery(this).attr('href').replace('origin', '');
                 var path = window.location.pathname;
 
                 jQuery(this).attr('href', oldHref + path);
             })
         }
     }
 
     function insertSubject() {
         if (jQuery('.betreff').length) {
             var input = jQuery('.betreff > input');
 			
             var origin = toTitleCase(window.location.hash.replace("#/", "").replace(/\//g, " » ").slice(0, -3).replace( /\%20/g , ' ' ));
 
             input.val(origin);
         }
 
     }
 
     function toTitleCase(str) {
         return str.replace(/\w\S*/g, function(txt){return txt.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + txt.substr(1).toLowerCase();});
     }
   </script>
